Pricing Notes and Assumptions:
1. The above pricing (excluding Add-Ons) are one-year terms, Add-Ons will be prorated if
purchased during the term.
2. The ThreatBoard - Base initiation does not include any customer branding, process
workflows, or additional APIs.
3. ThreatBoard is a software as a service (SaaS) and is hosted specifically from a secure
Peraton managed environment on behalf of its customer.
4. Renewal Term pricing is for one-year following the initial 2-year term.
5. Threatboard – Base subscriptions occur annually, and full payment of license will be due
at the time of Purchase Order.
6. Services for Software Licenses, Infrastructure Configuration, API Development, and
Compute Capacity will be paid annually, and full payment will be due at the time of
Purchase Order.
7. Add-On ThreatBoard users, storage or compute will be pro-rated during the term of the
ThreatBoard Subscription.
8. Add-on Professional Services will be Time & Material (T&M) paid monthly based on the
hours consumed.
9. The appropriate terms and conditions for the ThreatBoard - Base are located in the
corresponding Attachment L Solution.
10.Customer is required to setup a VPN connection to ThreatBoard for their users.
11.Users will only have access to platform and associated data during a paid subscription.
12.Peraton will not retain access or associated data after license has ended.
13.Customers cannot share access to ThreatBoard-Base with other state organizations.
14.Client network configuration and troubleshooting are outside the scope of Peraton
support for any infrastructure sitting outside of the Peraton hosted environment.
15.The ThreatBoard - Base pricing includes the following:
• A customer kick-off to provide access and orientation to the ThreatBoard platform.
• Access for up to 6 named users on the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform.
• User manuals and product documentation for the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard
platform.
• Maintenance and support of the Peraton-hosted Threatboard v1.0 application,
including:
o System Configuration
▪ Onboarding users; configuring roles and authorities as defined by the customer in
Section 2. 3 below.
▪ Integration of customer data sources that are supported by existing APIs. Currently
supported APIs include: AlienVault, Analyst1, Anomali, ARIN Whois, ATT&CK,
BlockCYpher, Carbon Black, CVE, Dragos, Insight VM, KEV, Hybrid Analysis,
RFP No.: 24-43230000-RFP-2 Page 23 of 24

## Page 24

Docusign Envelope ID: 1CC1F01E-7BAB-4EB7-B22B-5064B7EEE8F8
MalwareBazaar, MISP, NESSUS, OpenCTI, RiskIQ, Shodan, SNOW, Splunk,
Vectra.ai, Virus Total.
▪ Implementing playbooks as defined by the customer.
o System Maintenance and upgrades
▪ Maintenance of Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform and associated
Cloud/Infrastructure management.
▪ ThreatBoard version updates as available. All version updates will be communicated
with the customer and scheduled as to be minimally impactful to operations.
o Training and support
▪ In addition to documentation referenced above, Peraton will provide remote training
and on-call technical support to assist in tool usage.
▪ Support for the Peraton hosted ThreatBoard solution will be available via telephone
between 9am-5pm Eastern time, Monday through Friday.
o All combined forms of configuration, maintenance, training, and/or support are
not to exceed 100 hours per month. Hours do not roll-over month-to-month.
Customer may purchase additional support per established contract.

Pricing Notes and Assumptions:
1. The above pricing (excluding Add-Ons) are one-year terms, Add-Ons will be prorated if
purchased during the term.
2. The ThreatBoard - Base initiation does not include any customer branding, process
workflows, or additional APIs.
3. ThreatBoard is a software as a service (SaaS) and is hosted specifically from a secure
Peraton managed environment on behalf of its customer.
4. Renewal Term pricing is for one-year following the initial 2-year term.
5. Threatboard – Base subscriptions occur annually, and full payment of license will be due
at the time of Purchase Order.
6. Services for Software Licenses, Infrastructure Configuration, API Development, and
Compute Capacity will be paid annually, and full payment will be due at the time of
Purchase Order.
7. Add-On ThreatBoard users, storage or compute will be pro-rated during the term of the
ThreatBoard Subscription.
8. Add-on Professional Services will be Time & Material (T&M) paid monthly based on the
hours consumed.
9. The appropriate terms and conditions for the ThreatBoard - Base are located in the
corresponding Attachment L Solution.
10. Customer is required to setup a VPN connection to ThreatBoard for their users.
11. Users will only have access to platform and associated data during a paid subscription.
12. Peraton will not retain access or associated data after license has ended.
13. Customers cannot share access to ThreatBoard-Base with other state organizations.
14. Client network configuration and troubleshooting are outside the scope of Peraton
support for any infrastructure sitting outside of the Peraton hosted environment.
15. The ThreatBoard - Base pricing includes the following:
• A customer kick-off to provide access and orientation to the ThreatBoard platform.
• Access for up to 6 named users on the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform.
• User manuals and product documentation for the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard
platform.
• Maintenance and support of the Peraton-hosted Threatboard v1.0 application,
including:
o System Configuration
▪ Onboarding users; configuring roles and authorities as defined by the customer in
Section 2. 3 below.
▪ Integration of customer data sources that are supported by existing APIs. Currently
supported APIs include: AlienVault, Analyst1, Anomali, ARIN Whois, ATT&CK,
BlockCYpher, Carbon Black, CVE, Dragos, Insight VM, KEV, Hybrid Analysis,
RFP No.: 24-43230000-RFP-2 Page 23 of 24

MalwareBazaar, MISP, NESSUS, OpenCTI, RiskIQ, Shodan, SNOW, Splunk,
Vectra.ai, Virus Total.
▪ Implementing playbooks as defined by the customer.
o System Maintenance and upgrades
▪ Maintenance of Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform and associated
Cloud/Infrastructure management.
▪ ThreatBoard version updates as available. All version updates will be communicated
with the customer and scheduled as to be minimally impactful to operations.
o Training and support
▪ In addition to documentation referenced above, Peraton will provide remote training
and on-call technical support to assist in tool usage.
▪ Support for the Peraton hosted ThreatBoard solution will be available via telephone
between 9am-5pm Eastern time, Monday through Friday.
o All combined forms of configuration, maintenance, training, and/or support are
not to exceed 100 hours per month. Hours do not roll-over month-to-month.
Customer may purchase additional support per established contract.

Pricing Notes and Assumptions:
1. The above pricing (excluding Add-Ons) are one-year terms, Add-Ons will be prorated if
purchased during the term.
2. The ThreatBoard - Base initiation does not include any customer branding, process
workflows, or additional APIs.
3. ThreatBoard is a software as a service (SaaS) and is hosted specifically from a secure
Peraton managed environment on behalf of its customer.
4. Renewal Term pricing is for one-year following the initial 2-year term.
5. Threatboard – Base subscriptions occur annually, and full payment of license will be due
at the time of Purchase Order.
6. Services for Software Licenses, Infrastructure Configuration, API Development, and
Compute Capacity will be paid annually, and full payment will be due at the time of
Purchase Order.
7. Add-On ThreatBoard users, storage or compute will be pro-rated during the term of the
ThreatBoard Subscription.
8. Add-on Professional Services will be Time & Material (T&M) paid monthly based on the
hours consumed.
9. The appropriate terms and conditions for the ThreatBoard - Base are located in the
corresponding Attachment L Solution.
10. Customer is required to setup a VPN connection to ThreatBoard for their users.
11. Users will only have access to platform and associated data during a paid subscription.
12. Peraton will not retain access or associated data after license has ended.
13. Customers cannot share access to ThreatBoard-Base with other state organizations.
14. Client network configuration and troubleshooting are outside the scope of Peraton
support for any infrastructure sitting outside of the Peraton hosted environment.
15. The ThreatBoard - Base pricing includes the following:
• A customer kick-off to provide access and orientation to the ThreatBoard platform.
• Access for up to 6 named users on the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform.
• User manuals and product documentation for the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard
platform.
• Maintenance and support of the Peraton-hosted Threatboard v1.0 application,
including:
o System Configuration
▪ Onboarding users; configuring roles and authorities as defined by the customer in
Section 2. 3 below.
▪ Integration of customer data sources that are supported by existing APIs. Currently
supported APIs include: AlienVault, Analyst1, Anomali, ARIN Whois, ATT&CK,
BlockCYpher, Carbon Black, CVE, Dragos, Insight VM, KEV, Hybrid Analysis,
RFP No.: 24-43230000-RFP-2 Page 23 of 24

▪ Implementing playbooks as defined by the customer.

▪ In addition to documentation referenced above, Peraton will provide remote training
and on-call technical support to assist in tool usage.
▪ Support for the Peraton hosted ThreatBoard solution will be available via telephone
between 9am-5pm Eastern time, Monday through Friday.
o All combined forms of configuration, maintenance, training, and/or support are
not to exceed 100 hours per month. Hours do not roll-over month-to-month.
Customer may purchase additional support per established contract.

Pricing Notes and Assumptions:
1. The above pricing (excluding Add-Ons) are one-year terms, Add-Ons will be prorated if
purchased during the term.
2. The ThreatBoard - Base initiation does not include any customer branding, process
workflows, or additional APIs.
3. ThreatBoard is a software as a service (SaaS) and is hosted specifically from a secure
Peraton managed environment on behalf of its customer.
4. Renewal Term pricing is for one-year following the initial 2-year term.
5. Threatboard – Base subscriptions occur annually, and full payment of license will be due
at the time of Purchase Order.
6. Services for Software Licenses, Infrastructure Configuration, API Development, and
Compute Capacity will be paid annually, and full payment will be due at the time of
Purchase Order.
7. Add-On ThreatBoard users, storage or compute will be pro-rated during the term of the
ThreatBoard Subscription.
8. Add-on Professional Services will be Time & Material (T&M) paid monthly based on the
hours consumed.
9. The appropriate terms and conditions for the ThreatBoard - Base are located in the
corresponding Attachment L Solution.
10. Customer is required to setup a VPN connection to ThreatBoard for their users.
11. Users will only have access to platform and associated data during a paid subscription.
12. Peraton will not retain access or associated data after license has ended.
13. Customers cannot share access to ThreatBoard-Base with other state organizations.
14. Client network configuration and troubleshooting are outside the scope of Peraton
support for any infrastructure sitting outside of the Peraton hosted environment.
15. The ThreatBoard - Base pricing includes the following:
• A customer kick-off to provide access and orientation to the ThreatBoard platform.
• Access for up to 6 named users on the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard platform.
• User manuals and product documentation for the Peraton-hosted ThreatBoard
platform.
• Maintenance and support of the Peraton-hosted Threatboard v1.0 application,
including:
o System Configuration
▪ Onboarding users; configuring roles and authorities as defined by the customer in
Section 2. 3 below.
▪ Integration of customer data sources that are supported by existing APIs. Currently
